            "title": "如何打造颜值与实用兼具的玄关？", 
            "content": "<p></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-935f0847309bae0a253577b94efd1e4a_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1920\" data-rawheight=\"600\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1920\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-935f0847309bae0a253577b94efd1e4a_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1920&#39; height=&#39;600&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1920\" data-rawheight=\"600\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1920\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-935f0847309bae0a253577b94efd1e4a_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-935f0847309bae0a253577b94efd1e4a_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>玄关，是进出门的必经之所，是从繁杂的室外区域进入一个家的最初感觉；作为家给人带来的第一印象，玄关设计尤为重要。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-eb3123f3128b82b036a69e587048530c_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1620\" data-rawheight=\"1080\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1620\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-eb3123f3128b82b036a69e587048530c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1620&#39; height=&#39;1080&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1620\" data-rawheight=\"1080\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1620\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-eb3123f3128b82b036a69e587048530c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-eb3123f3128b82b036a69e587048530c_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>颜值与实用并存的玄关设计，能让我们一回家就能够卸下伪装，消除疲惫，以真实放松的状态享受家的温暖。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-4ea25c729b74603949f6df1dd33aa7eb_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"846\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-4ea25c729b74603949f6df1dd33aa7eb_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;846&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"846\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-4ea25c729b74603949f6df1dd33aa7eb_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-4ea25c729b74603949f6df1dd33aa7eb_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>那么如何打造颜值与实力兼具的玄关呢？</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><blockquote><b>1、玄关装饰要美观</b></blockquote><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>玄关设计是家居设计的一部分，因此其风格应与整个室内环境相和谐，起到承上启下的作用，玄关也是室内风格的一个缩影。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b9c3133bef53f018bc4faf7ca5fc4e6a_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"846\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b9c3133bef53f018bc4faf7ca5fc4e6a_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;846&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"846\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b9c3133bef53f018bc4faf7ca5fc4e6a_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b9c3133bef53f018bc4faf7ca5fc4e6a_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>打造美观的玄关，首先要注意不能杂乱，想要的越多，出来的效果越差！</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-84944940445d3864a098678e4e541344_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"778\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-84944940445d3864a098678e4e541344_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;778&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"778\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-84944940445d3864a098678e4e541344_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-84944940445d3864a098678e4e541344_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>统一的色调，会让玄关有伸展性；铺上一张呼应整体风格的地毯或者合适的地砖，空间更有层次感。当然也要考虑与室内风格协调，形成良好的衔接，美观实用。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5997195e3fd758a8915cc34bbfb6c20c_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1024\" data-rawheight=\"769\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1024\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5997195e3fd758a8915cc34bbfb6c20c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1024&#39; height=&#39;769&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1024\" data-rawheight=\"769\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1024\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5997195e3fd758a8915cc34bbfb6c20c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5997195e3fd758a8915cc34bbfb6c20c_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-c89282259c02ed3868ae830f69bec92a_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"600\" data-rawheight=\"841\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"600\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-c89282259c02ed3868ae830f69bec92a_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;600&#39; height=&#39;841&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"600\" data-rawheight=\"841\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"600\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-c89282259c02ed3868ae830f69bec92a_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-c89282259c02ed3868ae830f69bec92a_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>一张小小的玄关桌，其装饰性往往大于实用性，但它却是主人品味的缩影，值得我们好好花心思布置一番。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6bde52a420d3a42e74046912ff833b0e_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"428\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"428\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6bde52a420d3a42e74046912ff833b0e_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;428&#39; height=&#39;640&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"428\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"428\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6bde52a420d3a42e74046912ff833b0e_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6bde52a420d3a42e74046912ff833b0e_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>可以选择自己喜欢的摆件、鲜花放上，让劳累了一天的自己，进门的第一眼就能见到自己喜欢的物品，心情定会愉悦起来。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ac401804465bfaaf57bb9ab6f15d78e7_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"426\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"426\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ac401804465bfaaf57bb9ab6f15d78e7_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;426&#39; height=&#39;640&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"426\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"426\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ac401804465bfaaf57bb9ab6f15d78e7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ac401804465bfaaf57bb9ab6f15d78e7_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><blockquote><b>2、功能实用</b></blockquote><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>玄关的设计也要讲究实用性，大鞋柜的设置可以满足一家人的存放物品以及换鞋需求。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-a0e2b49a70a3908a754c5c64e10fb460_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"428\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-a0e2b49a70a3908a754c5c64e10fb460_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;428&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"428\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-a0e2b49a70a3908a754c5c64e10fb460_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-a0e2b49a70a3908a754c5c64e10fb460_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>对于小户型来说，玄关的面积有限（或者没有玄关空间），我们可以在玄关处放置一个收纳柜或者多层的架子，只选择几双经常穿的鞋子放在玄关，定时更换。学会做断舍离，才能打造有序的玄关。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5701728ebf1180c6f81855f0bc6428e8_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"426\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"426\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5701728ebf1180c6f81855f0bc6428e8_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;426&#39; height=&#39;640&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"426\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"426\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5701728ebf1180c6f81855f0bc6428e8_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5701728ebf1180c6f81855f0bc6428e8_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-3c335dc5a8802724e48bf03621fd9670_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"842\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-3c335dc5a8802724e48bf03621fd9670_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;842&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"842\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-3c335dc5a8802724e48bf03621fd9670_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-3c335dc5a8802724e48bf03621fd9670_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>衣帽架、大衣镜能让进出门更加方便。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-9ab2128a0aa4f79e869ad96dee7af2a4_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"846\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-9ab2128a0aa4f79e869ad96dee7af2a4_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;846&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"846\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-9ab2128a0aa4f79e869ad96dee7af2a4_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-9ab2128a0aa4f79e869ad96dee7af2a4_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-57cb6691d8d79ff537867caf66762561_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"900\" data-rawheight=\"500\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"900\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-57cb6691d8d79ff537867caf66762561_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;900&#39; height=&#39;500&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"900\" data-rawheight=\"500\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"900\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-57cb6691d8d79ff537867caf66762561_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-57cb6691d8d79ff537867caf66762561_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>考虑到下雨天会用伞，最好在玄关处放置一个雨伞桶，以免雨伞上的水滴得到处都是。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7f05ee3fa048a5ab5a0a857787593b9f_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"494\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"494\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7f05ee3fa048a5ab5a0a857787593b9f_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;494&#39; height=&#39;640&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"494\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"494\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7f05ee3fa048a5ab5a0a857787593b9f_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7f05ee3fa048a5ab5a0a857787593b9f_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><blockquote><b>3、考虑家庭成员的不同需求</b></blockquote><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>玄关设计也要考虑到家中常住人口的生活习惯。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-eaca51091e6415e4e295c0c056f509a7_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"426\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"426\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-eaca51091e6415e4e295c0c056f509a7_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;426&#39; height=&#39;640&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"426\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"426\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-eaca51091e6415e4e295c0c056f509a7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-eaca51091e6415e4e295c0c056f509a7_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>如果家中有小孩，设计时不妨将鞋柜的一部分分割成适合小孩身高的抽屉，培养孩子独立取换鞋的习惯。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-a7741e33ddb98139724d649179e0213a_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"788\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-a7741e33ddb98139724d649179e0213a_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;788&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"788\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-a7741e33ddb98139724d649179e0213a_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-a7741e33ddb98139724d649179e0213a_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>频繁弯腰/起身取放物品，以及站着换鞋，会给老人的身体增加一定负担，这时候就需要一个小小的换鞋凳。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-d98a45231c993d7f0fda442f83496793_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"512\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"512\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-d98a45231c993d7f0fda442f83496793_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;512&#39; height=&#39;640&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"512\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"512\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-d98a45231c993d7f0fda442f83496793_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-d98a45231c993d7f0fda442f83496793_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-19c64b8b848dd8be031ad15aac18df96_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"415\" data-rawheight=\"560\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"415\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;415&#39; height=&#39;560&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"415\" data-rawheight=\"560\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"415\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-19c64b8b848dd8be031ad15aac18df96_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><blockquote><b>4、尺子小结</b></blockquote><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>玄关是连接室外不室内的过渡空间，考虑到秋冬季当天外套的收纳，其深度在<b>550mm——600mm</b>最为合适。</p><p>另外，如果鞋柜没设计好，高度做高了，这种小小的上下鞋架，可以将鞋子上下叠放起来。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6a3b05b65fc6dddb6eb09ece1c9a7fae_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"633\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6a3b05b65fc6dddb6eb09ece1c9a7fae_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;633&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"633\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6a3b05b65fc6dddb6eb09ece1c9a7fae_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6a3b05b65fc6dddb6eb09ece1c9a7fae_b.jpg\"/></figure><p></p><p></p>",

width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;564&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"564\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-983cac9b43b432cc7808a2aae85aaee6_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-983cac9b43b432cc7808a2aae85aaee6_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-1ce59ac5a7e7df06c675204805ca1319_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"557\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-1ce59ac5a7e7df06c675204805ca1319_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;750&#39; height=&#39;557&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"557\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-1ce59ac5a7e7df06c675204805ca1319_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-1ce59ac5a7e7df06c675204805ca1319_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>②立体感更强，弥补乳胶漆、壁纸等传统墙面装饰材料平面、单调以及传统壁纸易剥落、起皮、开裂等情况。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-43b8f14b7f2516871e088bcf240a6d7c_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"320\" data-rawheight=\"480\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"320\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;320&#39; height=&#39;480&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"320\" data-rawheight=\"480\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"320\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-43b8f14b7f2516871e088bcf240a6d7c_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>缺点：</p><p>①与普通的乳胶漆或壁纸相比，艺术涂料施工的技术含量更高，需要具备较高的施工水平跟审美的专业的施工人员。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2242881225819914b12ae7a2bf151c6c_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"450\" data-rawheight=\"308\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"450\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2242881225819914b12ae7a2bf151c6c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;450&#39; height=&#39;308&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"450\" data-rawheight=\"308\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"450\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2242881225819914b12ae7a2bf151c6c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2242881225819914b12ae7a2bf151c6c_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><h2><b>二、石材电视背景</b></h2><p><b>推荐指数：</b>★★★★</p><p>在时尚现代的装修风格里，简洁大气的石材电视背景墙是比较常用的设计元素。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7894b4438117836ff595c303747e20b3_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"423\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7894b4438117836ff595c303747e20b3_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;423&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"423\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7894b4438117836ff595c303747e20b3_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7894b4438117836ff595c303747e20b3_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>优点：</b></p><p>①大理石天然纹理装饰，富有质感，空间显得干净利落，视觉体验非常舒适。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-d1da9ca0fc9edb55db3ef0de84dbee9f_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"335\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-d1da9ca0fc9edb55db3ef0de84dbee9f_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;335&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"335\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-d1da9ca0fc9edb55db3ef0de84dbee9f_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-d1da9ca0fc9edb55db3ef0de84dbee9f_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>②石材背景墙经久耐用，集防火、防潮、防噪音于一身，且易于清洁。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b24dfebcb47a047371af7bef6ec48544_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1198\" data-rawheight=\"741\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1198\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b24dfebcb47a047371af7bef6ec48544_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;338&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"338\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b6fdc00653a2cabfe7e376cec0727a18_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b6fdc00653a2cabfe7e376cec0727a18_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>②重量大，需要用龙骨固定，安装、改换难度比较大。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6370352ecbc2f7d75b7c7e4a838733d5_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1211\" data-rawheight=\"810\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1211\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6370352ecbc2f7d75b7c7e4a838733d5_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1211&#39; height=&#39;810&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1211\" data-rawheight=\"810\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1211\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6370352ecbc2f7d75b7c7e4a838733d5_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6370352ecbc2f7d75b7c7e4a838733d5_b.jpg\"/></figure><h2><b>三、电视背景墙柜</b></h2><p><b>推荐指数：</b>★★★★★</p><p>有时候，电视背景墙除了考虑整体视觉效果之外，还会承担一些其他功能，比如小户型收纳不足。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-12f5ef7e4decc2a03b8c7f1ddccc22fc_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"752\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-12f5ef7e4decc2a03b8c7f1ddccc22fc_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;752&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"752\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-12f5ef7e4decc2a03b8c7f1ddccc22fc_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-12f5ef7e4decc2a03b8c7f1ddccc22fc_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>优点：</b></p><p>①通过定制柜体，背景墙与柜子结合，将墙壁空间最大化利用起来，这样的设计方式让客厅收纳大幅度扩容。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3082d4ae176416f717bb7ed1de9553e6_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"423\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3082d4ae176416f717bb7ed1de9553e6_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;423&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"423\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3082d4ae176416f717bb7ed1de9553e6_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3082d4ae176416f717bb7ed1de9553e6_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>缺点：</b></p><p>①占领一定的客厅活动空间</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-0597af07bd049b57500e5d11227528ae_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"571\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-0597af07bd049b57500e5d11227528ae_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;571&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"571\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-0597af07bd049b57500e5d11227528ae_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-0597af07bd049b57500e5d11227528ae_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>客厅电视背景墙应该注意一下几点：</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>1、尺寸选择。</p><p>眼睛距离电视机的最佳距离应当是电视机尺寸的3.5倍，通过测量墙体的长度和高度，同时考虑到扣除空调位置，吊顶高度，确定电视背景墙的长度和高度。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3082d4ae176416f717bb7ed1de9553e6_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"423\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3082d4ae176416f717bb7ed1de9553e6_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;423&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"423\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3082d4ae176416f717bb7ed1de9553e6_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3082d4ae176416f717bb7ed1de9553e6_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>2、插座线路。</p><p>设计背景墙时，要在墙面留出足够的插座位置以及结实的基层。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-d25e2e3a8e32c10a3d2ddfac15c6ac6a_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"960\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"960\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-d25e2e3a8e32c10a3d2ddfac15c6ac6a_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;             "content": "<p>在<a href=\"https://zhuanlan.zhihu.com/p/38356788\" class=\"internal\">《还在为电视背景墙发愁？给你三款金牌推荐》</a>这篇文章中，我们给大家推荐了三款常用的电视背景墙，其实在布置家居的时候，我们的思维很容易形成定势，比如：客厅的配置基本上都是沙发+茶几+电视墙的组合，近年来，手机、电脑的功能逐渐取代电视，即使一年也开不了几次电视，却非要设计一个华丽气派却占空间的电视墙。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>谁说客厅就一定要电视+背景墙+茶几这种标配了？</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>设计的初始点是生活，所以重点是住的舒适。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>现如今我们的生活习惯发生了翻天覆地的变化，电视的刚需功能也伴随着新媒体的冲击变得越来越弱，逐渐被电脑、手机、IPAD、投影仪等设备取代。因此作为家庭核心区的客厅也应该有更多的可能。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>那么，没有电视的客厅应该如何设计呢？今天小尺就为大家提供几种其他客厅设计的可能性：</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><h2><b>壁炉型客厅</b></h2><p>在一些北欧风、美式风的设计里，经常会看到有壁炉的存在。正所谓围炉夜话，和家人一起坐在客厅里围着壁炉谈天说地，也能为整个客厅空间增添出几分装饰效果。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-1ce3967eb0019ef164b99a6cb3c2601b_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1242\" data-rawheight=\"1052\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1242\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-1ce3967eb0019ef164b99a6cb3c2601b_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;426&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"426\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-e4a5224a1d095b52312828bcf0d40708_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-e4a5224a1d095b52312828bcf0d40708_b.jpg\"/></figure><h2><b>家庭影院</b></h2><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>厌倦了千篇一律的电视背景墙，投影仪是不错的替代品，不用的时候收上去，还能省出一面墙的空间，即使是普通家庭，也能打造家庭影院般感觉。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-00e4e55bb4e7605bf02b6febb2324b29_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"560\" data-rawheight=\"560\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"560\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-00e4e55bb4e7605bf02b6febb2324b29_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;             "content": "<figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-dc9b68881ede736f80b0024a8841c647_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"950\" data-rawheight=\"633\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"950\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-dc9b68881ede736f80b0024a8841c647_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;950&#39; height=&#39;633&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"950\" data-rawheight=\"633\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"950\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-dc9b68881ede736f80b0024a8841c647_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-dc9b68881ede736f80b0024a8841c647_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>很多喜欢简约风格家居的人，在装修时选择了刷大白墙，但是住的久了，难免会觉得太单调了，尤其是采光不好的户型，更会显得清冷压抑。</p><p>如果并不准备对大白墙进行大的改造，那么就要靠软装的魅力来拯救大白墙啦。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><blockquote><b>灯光</b></blockquote><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>灯光是营造室内氛围的利器，大白墙过于冰冷，那就用暖色的灯光来调节。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-3428d93e461ad2a1f21af901a746ae5c_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"474\" data-rawheight=\"474\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"474\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-3428d93e461ad2a1f21af901a746ae5c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;474&#39; height=&#39;474&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"474\" data-rawheight=\"474\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"474\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-3428d93e461ad2a1f21af901a746ae5c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-3428d93e461ad2a1f21af901a746ae5c_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>现代家居中不仅是主灯光源，还有射灯、筒灯、灯带等等辅助光源，利用好这些往往能让大白墙变得有层次感。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-224ca6cc0901f5e2b955d0752801f145_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"705\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-224ca6cc0901f5e2b955d0752801f145_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;705&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"705\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-224ca6cc0901f5e2b955d0752801f145_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-224ca6cc0901f5e2b955d0752801f145_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><blockquote><b>装饰画、小贴纸</b></blockquote><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>嫌大白墙过于单调，装饰画与白墙简直是标配，有了装饰画的点缀，大白墙瞬间就能增添活力。不同的装饰画所营造的家居氛围也不一样，所以要挑选适合自己家的装饰画。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5f3e6496041f7ebf25a0177fabeac6af_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"632\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5f3e6496041f7ebf25a0177fabeac6af_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;632&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"632\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5f3e6496041f7ebf25a0177fabeac6af_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5f3e6496041f7ebf25a0177fabeac6af_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>也可以将自己的旅行照、家人合照打印出来挂在墙上，对这个家也会更有归属感。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-8d47c519006e0aa993570fc755ddf856_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"448\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"448\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-8d47c519006e0aa993570fc755ddf856_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;448&#39; height=&#39;640&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"448\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"448\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-8d47c519006e0aa993570fc755ddf856_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-8d47c519006e0aa993570fc755ddf856_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>觉得挑选装饰画太麻烦？简单的小贴纸也能提升白墙的温度，看厌了，随时可以改换。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-a485e8c81fc851f159077d9a527c4d10_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"542\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-a485e8c81fc851f159077d9a527c4d10_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;800&#39; height=&#39;542&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"542\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-a485e8c81fc851f159077d9a527c4d10_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-a485e8c81fc851f159077d9a527c4d10_b.jpg\"/></figure><blockquote><b>隔板、置物架</b></blockquote><p>隔板与置物架在丰满空间的同时，还能打造出看似简单却有着功能性的空间。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-cd58623ff6aaf5d800af7efb0bd9f386_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"478\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-cd58623ff6aaf5d800af7efb0bd9f386_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;478&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"478\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-cd58623ff6aaf5d800af7efb0bd9f386_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-cd58623ff6aaf5d800af7efb0bd9f386_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-8211f55507130b42d4e346bdadbebde9_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"846\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-8211f55507130b42d4e346bdadbebde9_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;             "content": "<p>要使衣柜的使用方式尽量适合人体的自然形态，让我们用得更加舒适，这就在尺寸上有一定的要求。</p><p>根据我国国家标准GB3327-82规定，<b>标准的衣柜尺寸</b>包括一下几点（以下尺度单位均统一为毫米mm）：</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-017dad6d4fc83008c931439ccb857806_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"555\" data-rawheight=\"178\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"555\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-017dad6d4fc83008c931439ccb857806_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;555&#39; height=&#39;178&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"555\" data-rawheight=\"178\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"555\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-017dad6d4fc83008c931439ccb857806_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-017dad6d4fc83008c931439ccb857806_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>当然在实际运用中，不同的厂家设计的尺寸也会有所出入，所以我们在选择衣柜时，也要考虑好自己的使用的方便性，选择合适的衣柜。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>为方便每一个家庭成员拿取衣物，我们以女主人为例，<b>A小姐的身高是160㎝，</b>那么她举起手臂时能够到的最大高度是1900mm，因此衣柜的最<b>上层隔板最好不要超过2000mm</b>，衣柜的顶部高度最好<b>不超过2400mm</b>。</p><p>提醒：下柜做得太高的话，对门板的要求很高，久了变形的可能性要增大很多，太矮的话就比门还要矮了，不是很好看。</p><p>除了衣柜的整体尺寸外，衣柜的每个<b>收纳空间</b>也是有尺寸上的讲究的，具体可划分为被褥区、上衣区、长衣区、挂裤区、叠放区及抽屉等，每一区域根据存储功能的不同，都有不同的尺寸要求：</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-93da435a8208b3167c3ed0bface867d5_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"611\" data-rawheight=\"264\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"611\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-93da435a8208b3167c3ed0bface867d5_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;611&#39; height=&#39;264&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"611\" data-rawheight=\"264\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"611\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-93da435a8208b3167c3ed0bface867d5_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-93da435a8208b3167c3ed0bface867d5_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5c5fe25253542cfad6ba8cd0f0c9861f_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1013\" data-rawheight=\"450\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1013\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5c5fe25253542cfad6ba8cd0f0c9861f_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1013&#39; height=&#39;450&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1013\" data-rawheight=\"450\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1013\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5c5fe25253542cfad6ba8cd0f0c9861f_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5c5fe25253542cfad6ba8cd0f0c9861f_b.jpg\"/></figure><blockquote>需提醒大家的是：<br/>上衣区的高度可根据使用者的身高、衣服长度做一定调整，上衣的衣摆最好距离底部8厘米，下方空余的地方还可以叠放一些衣物。</blockquote><p>柜设计的合理不合理，很大程度上取决于衣柜的尺寸是否合理，在做到了解尺寸外，还要根据卧室内的实际情况调整，让家中的衣柜兼具收纳和美观，使用更方便。</p>",

            "upvote": 2, 
            "title": "面对室内甲醛污染，我们如何自救？", 
            "content": "<p>最近自如房甲醛超标的事件闹得人心惶惶，装修污染问题一直是我们所关注的，他会直接影响我们的身体健康。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f4c361e9b1c8959d91b634aa167a39c5_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"850\" data-rawheight=\"500\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"850\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f4c361e9b1c8959d91b634aa167a39c5_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;850&#39; height=&#39;500&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"850\" data-rawheight=\"500\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"850\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f4c361e9b1c8959d91b634aa167a39c5_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f4c361e9b1c8959d91b634aa167a39c5_b.jpg\"/></figure><h2><b>那么甲醛超标会对我们的身体造成怎样的影响呢：</b></h2><p>甲醛超标不仅会引起<b>咽喉不适，诱发鼻咽癌</b>，长时间吸入还会导致<b>白血病</b>。</p><p>而在日常生活中，我们接触的甲醛主要来自于家庭装修，墙面涂料、装修板材，家具中的胶黏剂以及窗帘、地毯等纺织品在制造的过程中使用的防燃材料，都会有一定的甲醛成分。</p><p>很多人认为家里闻不到气味，就代表没有甲醛，其实是错误的。</p><p>甲醛是有特殊刺激气味的无色气体，它的释放是一个缓慢并且持续的过程。</p><p>通常各种家具、建材在打开包装后的<b>3至6个月内</b>，甲醛的释放量会达到峰值。其中窗帘等纺织品产生的游离甲醛最少需要<b>两个月</b>的时间挥发。</p><p>当然，除了甲醛以外，家装中其他污染源也不可小觑。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-5c2efab91c60d8422f44082a4b57bdce_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"931\" data-rawheight=\"595\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"931\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-5c2efab91c60d8422f44082a4b57bdce_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;931&#39; height=&#39;595&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"931\" data-rawheight=\"595\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"931\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-5c2efab91c60d8422f44082a4b57bdce_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-5c2efab91c60d8422f44082a4b57bdce_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>其中，在室内装饰过程中，TVOC主要来自油漆，涂料和胶粘剂。正常情况下，室内TVOC浓度通常在0.2mg/m3到2mg/m3之间，而在不当装修施工中，甚至可高出数十倍。它在国际癌症研究机构中与甲醛都同属1类强致癌物质。</p><h2><b>那么该怎样去甲醛（装修污染），保证室内空气安全呢？</b></h2><p><b>控制原材料</b></p><p>了解室内甲醛的来源后，尽可能使用环保乳胶漆和板材，减少甲醛产生，这才是从根本上解决问题的方法。当然将产生甲醛的家具先放在阳台处通通风，移除释放源，也是不错的做法。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-df42c505255e75f631fe84095ba35eb8_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1000\" data-rawheight=\"1499\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1000\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-df42c505255e75f631fe84095ba35eb8_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1000&#39; height=&#39;1499&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1000\" data-rawheight=\"1499\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1000\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-df42c505255e75f631fe84095ba35eb8_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-df42c505255e75f631fe84095ba35eb8_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>开窗透气法</b></p><p>开窗透气是最经济便捷的去甲醛方法了，装修完后，打开柜子，开窗透气；但是这种方法也有一定的<b>弊端</b>：</p><p>①开窗会导致气流紊乱，可能把卫生间和厨房的异味带入客厅和卧室；</p><p>②室外空气夹带大量室外的尘埃，影响室内清洁卫生；</p><p>③无法避免的噪音污染</p><p>④采暖会造成大量的能源、电量的浪费</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-323cdee1dff06724bfff9c1154a12e19_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"1200\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-323cdee1dff06724bfff9c1154a12e19_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;800&#39; height=&#39;1200&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"1200\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-323cdee1dff06724bfff9c1154a12e19_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-323cdee1dff06724bfff9c1154a12e19_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>植物净化</b></p><p>用植物和竹炭确实可以吸入甲醛，可是效率很低，而且如果把吸饱了甲醛的竹炭放到没有甲醛污染的空房间里，附着在上面的甲醛反而会迅速释放；用醋蒸和放橘子皮，就完全是障眼法了，靠遮住甲醛的气味自我安慰。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7557f88110313924e5cf934384ffde0b_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"915\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"915\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7557f88110313924e5cf934384ffde0b_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;915&#39; height=&#39;640&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"915\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"915\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7557f88110313924e5cf934384ffde0b_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7557f88110313924e5cf934384ffde0b_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>活性炭吸附</b></p><p>活性炭作为一种吸附材料，能够减轻一定的装修污染。但是活性炭只能单一吸附，无法分解、消耗所吸附的有害物质，在使用一段时间后，活性炭就会饱和。饱和的活性炭如果不及时更换，也会将吸附的装修污染物排到室内，刚装修好的房子装修污染比较重，一般来说<b>20天-30天</b>就需要更换活性炭包。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-328f319fa1426b2f36da45020ef211a9_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1023\" data-rawheight=\"690\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1023\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-328f319fa1426b2f36da45020ef211a9_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1023&#39; height=&#39;690&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1023\" data-rawheight=\"690\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1023\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-328f319fa1426b2f36da45020ef211a9_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-328f319fa1426b2f36da45020ef211a9_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>新风系统</b></p><p>新风系统遵循自然通风原理得原理，用室外的新鲜空气更新室内由于居住及生活过程而污染了的空气，以保持室内空气的洁净度达到某一最低标准的水平。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-837ec4d6dd4e5c4354c791cc56b0ddd7_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1054\" data-rawheight=\"636\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1054\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-837ec4d6dd4e5c4354c791cc56b0ddd7_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1054&#39; height=&#39;636&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1054\" data-rawheight=\"636\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1054\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-837ec4d6dd4e5c4354c791cc56b0ddd7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-837ec4d6dd4e5c4354c791cc56b0ddd7_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>新风系统通过不断的送风、回风，可以把室内污染空气包括甲醛不断排出去，把室外空气经过清洁处理后源源不断送入室内，不停循环运行，能够有效<b>稀释</b>室内家具等会发出来的甲醛。安装了新风系统就相当于给房子装了一个绿色的“肺”。</p>",

            "upvote": 0, 
            "title": "厨房装修需要注意哪些细节？", 
            "content": "<h2><b>水电</b></h2><p>厨房因为大功率电器比较多，水电需要再装修前规划好，不要让几个大功率的电器共用一个插座（尤其是冰箱，最好单独使用插座），还要做好电路保护装置，避免造成电路隐患。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-035ae62d83474983de39fa57b290e25f_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1200\" data-rawheight=\"809\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1200\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-035ae62d83474983de39fa57b290e25f_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1200&#39; height=&#39;809&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1200\" data-rawheight=\"809\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1200\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-035ae62d83474983de39fa57b290e25f_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-035ae62d83474983de39fa57b290e25f_b.jpg\"/></figure><h2><b>吊顶</b></h2><p>厨房一定要吊顶，因为中式家庭厨房以烹炒为主，烟熏火燎，长期下来厨房装修材料容易老化，发黄。另外，要记得在吊顶上留个维修孔，便于日后损坏时维修，因为吊顶内除了有电线外，还有侦测烟雾设备、消防管线等。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6cea693ed4e25008339d22d3d130e186_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1200\" data-rawheight=\"800\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1200\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6cea693ed4e25008339d22d3d130e186_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1200&#39; height=&#39;800&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1200\" data-rawheight=\"800\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1200\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6cea693ed4e25008339d22d3d130e186_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6cea693ed4e25008339d22d3d130e186_b.jpg\"/></figure><h2><b>灯光</b></h2><p>厨房的灯光一定要明亮自然，主灯与辅助灯光相结合。因为吊柜可能会遮挡来自顶部的光线，所以建议在操作区安装局部照明。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-69239d62f6adabc6b8367894ddee311a_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1000\" data-rawheight=\"1400\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1000\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-69239d62f6adabc6b8367894ddee311a_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1000&#39; height=&#39;1400&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1000\" data-rawheight=\"1400\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1000\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-69239d62f6adabc6b8367894ddee311a_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-69239d62f6adabc6b8367894ddee311a_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>另外厨房油烟重，建议选用防尘、防火、易擦洗的灯具。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><h2><b>橱柜（操作台尺寸）</b></h2><p>操作区高度应根据家里常下厨的人的身高来确定，最理想的状态是<b>身高÷2+50㎜</b>，以A小姐为例，A小姐身高为1600mm，则她最舒适的操作高度为1600÷2+50=850mm。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2fa412e75e5460c92524051039eaf730_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"600\" data-rawheight=\"886\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"600\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2fa412e75e5460c92524051039eaf730_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;600&#39; height=&#39;886&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"600\" data-rawheight=\"886\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"600\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2fa412e75e5460c92524051039eaf730_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2fa412e75e5460c92524051039eaf730_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>对于烹饪区来说，最理想的状态是比操作区低100㎜，即750㎜对A小姐来说是最合适的炒菜高度。</p><p>传统橱柜水槽和其他区域都是850mm，在用水洗菜和餐盘时，实际的操作高度只有650mm，长时间的弯腰作业会很疲惫。只有当水槽高度在900mm—950mm左右时，使用水槽才会觉得轻松。</p><p>单独加高水槽价格偏高，可以将水槽部分的地柜整体加高节约成本。</p><p>另外橱柜台面最好选择防水、防火、易清洁的材料，橱柜背面加一个挡水板，高出台面一点，可以防止水流到橱柜后面，损坏橱柜。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><h2><b>地面</b></h2><p>厨房地面在选择瓷砖时，要注意防滑排水、方便清洁，建议安装地漏选用防滑砖，瓷砖缝隙最好小一点，好打理。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5921606cd5d52316e077724f24dd2ff4_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"577\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5921606cd5d52316e077724f24dd2ff4_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;800&#39; height=&#39;577&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"577\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5921606cd5d52316e077724f24dd2ff4_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5921606cd5d52316e077724f24dd2ff4_b.jpg\"/></figure><h2><b>油烟机</b></h2><p>油烟机的高度不能超过灶台700㎜，否则吸烟效果会大打折扣，另外高度太低又容易让做菜的人磕到头，因此建议选用侧吸式的油烟机。</p><p></p>",

            "upvote": 2, 
            "title": "阳台门怎么选？看下你家的户型适合哪种", 
            "content": "<p>家中的阳台连接着室内与室外，是一块多用途的空间，具有通风和采光的功能，但也成为灰尘进入室内的途径。而阳台门恰好能阻隔灰尘，即使是封闭阳台，从安全角度考虑也很有必要。</p><p>那么应该选择什么样的阳台门呢？</p><h2><b>类型</b></h2><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><blockquote><b>推拉门</b></blockquote><p>优点：节省空间，美观</p><p>缺点：推拉轨道容易积攒灰尘，难清理，隔音较弱</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-c3b6e331b860d954c6e40d2a18f1684b_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"600\" data-rawheight=\"892\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"600\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-c3b6e331b860d954c6e40d2a18f1684b_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;600&#39; height=&#39;892&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"600\" data-rawheight=\"892\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"600\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-c3b6e331b860d954c6e40d2a18f1684b_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-c3b6e331b860d954c6e40d2a18f1684b_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-6d7c76f81bb905090af312e440dcb92f_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"1200\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-6d7c76f81bb905090af312e440dcb92f_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;800&#39; height=&#39;1200&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"1200\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-6d7c76f81bb905090af312e440dcb92f_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-6d7c76f81bb905090af312e440dcb92f_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4e2ff8a5cfdd95f1ad0a86a8510fe7e8_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"480\" data-rawheight=\"635\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"480\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4e2ff8a5cfdd95f1ad0a86a8510fe7e8_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;480&#39; height=&#39;635&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"480\" data-rawheight=\"635\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"480\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4e2ff8a5cfdd95f1ad0a86a8510fe7e8_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4e2ff8a5cfdd95f1ad0a86a8510fe7e8_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><blockquote><b>平开门</b></blockquote><p>优点：隔音较推拉门要更好，造价相对便宜</p><p>缺点：空间利用不如推拉门</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f839590ea8702fc29554ef8313db0013_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"600\" data-rawheight=\"750\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"600\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f839590ea8702fc29554ef8313db0013_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;600&#39; height=&#39;750&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"600\" data-rawheight=\"750\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"600\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f839590ea8702fc29554ef8313db0013_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f839590ea8702fc29554ef8313db0013_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-13e0c93589a41d027cd1e65a92995edf_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"736\" data-rawheight=\"1104\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"736\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-13e0c93589a41d027cd1e65a92995edf_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;736&#39; height=&#39;1104&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"736\" data-rawheight=\"1104\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"736\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-13e0c93589a41d027cd1e65a92995edf_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-13e0c93589a41d027cd1e65a92995edf_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-029796ed0bb4b7204f14302cb05f543a_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"600\" data-rawheight=\"400\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"600\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-029796ed0bb4b7204f14302cb05f543a_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;600&#39; height=&#39;400&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"600\" data-rawheight=\"400\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"600\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-029796ed0bb4b7204f14302cb05f543a_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-029796ed0bb4b7204f14302cb05f543a_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-fc392356135c4aeabb29f7b2b659c240_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"752\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-fc392356135c4aeabb29f7b2b659c240_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;752&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"752\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-fc392356135c4aeabb29f7b2b659c240_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-fc392356135c4aeabb29f7b2b659c240_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><blockquote><b>折叠门</b></blockquote><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>优点：美观新颖，比较灵活，相对平开门来说空间利用率更好；材质和样式多，可以根据个人爱好需求选择。</p><p>缺点：阳台处风出比较大，灰尘容易吸附到折叠门的角落或者缝隙里，不易打扫。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-0a5181d0d71dd7f417d485072fdade96_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"425\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-0a5181d0d71dd7f417d485072fdade96_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;425&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"425\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-0a5181d0d71dd7f417d485072fdade96_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-0a5181d0d71dd7f417d485072fdade96_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5e664ba2c11546827dbe0070094fb157_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"480\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5e664ba2c11546827dbe0070094fb157_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;480&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"480\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5e664ba2c11546827dbe0070094fb157_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5e664ba2c11546827dbe0070094fb157_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-e77de700e800308ff79f496bd3836ffc_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"1620\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-e77de700e800308ff79f496bd3836ffc_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;1620&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"1620\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-e77de700e800308ff79f496bd3836ffc_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-e77de700e800308ff79f496bd3836ffc_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>除了阳台门的类型，还需要材质上考虑，市面上主要有以下几种材质：</p><p><b>一、铝镁合金</b></p><p>铝镁合金材质的导热性能好，强度也达到了一定的程度，而且铝镁合金的外表是银白色的，比较美观。缺点就是不够耐磨，而且价格也较贵。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-13e0c93589a41d027cd1e65a92995edf_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"736\" data-rawheight=\"1104\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"736\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-13e0c93589a41d027cd1e65a92995edf_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;736&#39; height=&#39;1104&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"736\" data-rawheight=\"1104\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"736\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-13e0c93589a41d027cd1e65a92995edf_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-13e0c93589a41d027cd1e65a92995edf_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>二、钛镁合金材</b></p><p>钛镁合金材料比铝镁合金材料有了更强的硬度和导热性，当然价格也相对更贵一些。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-0b3d3f6a353194640b7fce98523f3eea_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"660\" data-rawheight=\"990\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"660\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-0b3d3f6a353194640b7fce98523f3eea_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;660&#39; height=&#39;990&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"660\" data-rawheight=\"990\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"660\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-0b3d3f6a353194640b7fce98523f3eea_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-0b3d3f6a353194640b7fce98523f3eea_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>三、木质</b></p><p>木质阳台推拉门主要是以实木为主，实木质地温润，与各类设计风格相搭都十分适宜，可以为家居增添优雅的氛围感。但是也有怕水、怕晒、脱色等缺点，不太推荐用在阳台移门上。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-8fb053f546785d367c47ad5ae47a2ad9_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"556\" data-rawheight=\"787\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"556\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-8fb053f546785d367c47ad5ae47a2ad9_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;556&#39; height=&#39;787&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"556\" data-rawheight=\"787\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"556\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-8fb053f546785d367c47ad5ae47a2ad9_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-8fb053f546785d367c47ad5ae47a2ad9_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>四、塑钢</b></p><p>这类材质密闭性及隔热性良好，还具有环保节能、隔音、美观、耐腐蚀、使用寿命长等优点。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b11b29df06ef317899b6418a1e7e0c9d_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"662\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b11b29df06ef317899b6418a1e7e0c9d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;500&#39; height=&#39;662&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"662\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b11b29df06ef317899b6418a1e7e0c9d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b11b29df06ef317899b6418a1e7e0c9d_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>小尺提醒大家：</p><p>不管是哪一种的材质，都有自己的优点和特性，具体还是要根据自身需求去选择。</p><p>如果对硬度强度没有什么要求的话，<b>塑钢是性价比较高的选择。</b></p><p>如果对隔音要求较高的话，推荐用塑钢推拉门。</p><p><b>如果牢固/耐用角度出发：钛镁合金＞铝镁合金＞塑钢＞木质</b></p><p>tips:<br/>1.考虑整体的协调性,例如:3米宽的阳台,那么阳台推拉门标准尺寸的高度一般在2.4米之内,太高的话会影响整体美观。<br/><br/>2.宽度：黄金尺寸在80厘米×200厘米左右,这个尺寸的门是比较稳固的。如果推拉门高于200cm,可以将推拉门的宽度缩窄,保持原有的门扇面积,这样做出的门的稳定性也可以相对保持。</p><p>3.厚度尺寸：如果阳台推拉门是采用玻璃或银镜做门芯的话,那么其厚度一般在5mm左右;如果阳台推拉门是采用木板做门芯的情况下,则其厚度一般选取10mm左右。</p>",
